  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageHamburgerMenu() {
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');
  var $navCloseBtn = $('#nav-close-btn');
  var $navToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--nav-toggle');

  function lockNavFocus() {
    $navCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusNavCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('masthead-nav'), event.target)) {
      $navCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockNavFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
    $navToggleBtn.focus();
  }

  // hamburger menu to toggle mobile nav, full screen hit area beneath
  // mobile nav to act as toggle target
  $navToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $nav.toggleClass('nav--is-open');
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockNavFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('masthead-nav');
      $nav.css('visibility', 'visible');
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockNavFocus();
        $navToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>
  <!--/.nav-->

  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageTipMenu() {
  var $tip = $('.js__tip');
  var $tipCloseBtn = $('#tip__btn-close');
  var $tipToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--tip-toggle');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockTipFocus() {
    $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusTipCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('tip'), event.target)) {
      $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockTipFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  // toggle tip full screen mobile menu
  $tipToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $tip.toggleClass('tip--is-open');
    if ($tip.hasClass('tip--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockTipFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('tip');
      $tip.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockTipFocus();
        $tipToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $tip.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>

          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/e6/4by3/2021/03/21/e6103dc7f6ac480db91c90e0fad13a19_md.jpg"/>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-82f7a2d1039b41bf80d3e00beb362bf0">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Rick Moranis
          </strong>
          seems to be wanted by the FBI for storming the Capitol -- at least that's what a lot of people are thinking based on photos the agency posted of the actual guy they're after.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-82f7a2d1039b41bf80d3e00beb362bf0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-62464295d78a4cfef3dedd945bfffd25">
         <p>
          Check out this dude that the FBI flagged and posted pics of on Sunday -- he's one of the several unidentified rioters who have since flown under the radar and escaped justice (for now) following the Jan. 6 insurrection. He's still out there, and Uncle Sam wants a chat.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-62464295d78a4cfef3dedd945bfffd25-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-db6a9ef800ae84ab889af6b4bc0e9152">
         <p>
          The feds need help finding him, so they threw up a digital WANTED poster, writing ... "You can help the #FBI identify individuals involved in the January 6
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/06/pro-trump-protesters-breach-storm-capitol-fight-dc-police-break-fence/">
           <strong>
            violence at the U.S. Capitol
           </strong>
          </a>
          . Visit http://tips.fbi.gov if you recognize this person. Reference photo 268 in your tip."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-db6a9ef800ae84ab889af6b4bc0e9152-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-1e87cbf62804f6a9d93b937d3440be8a">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/2a/4by3/2021/03/21/2a05c50263a34d8dbee477d4c846838f_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1e87cbf62804f6a9d93b937d3440be8a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a1818e5927d9a9cb32bd9b018414cef7">
         <p>
          While he isn't a dead ringer for Moranis, tons of folks think this man bears a passing resemblance -- and, sure, we can admit ... they look similar.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a1818e5927d9a9cb32bd9b018414cef7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0e984c43e498ed6ab714c87bea868e80">
         <p>
          The funny thing is ... Moranis is actually
          <a href="https://imgur.com/gallery/KPiH0om" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <strong>
            known for rocking helmets
           </strong>
          </a>
          throughout his film career, especially in his heyday back in the '80s and '90s. Here's a quick rundown of movies he's in where he wears helmets/hard hats -- 'Honey, I Shrunk the Kids,' 'Honey, I Blew Up the Kid,' 'Honey, We Shrank Ourselves,' 'Ghostbusters,' 'Strange Brew 1 &amp; 2,' 'Little Giants,' 'The Flintstones,' 'Big Bully' and of course ... the king of them all, 'Spaceballs'!!!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0e984c43e498ed6ab714c87bea868e80-->

         <p>
          Of course, we know that's not Rick ... and that the FBI isn't really looking for him. BUT, just to be accurate and to make sure we have all our ducks in a row here ... we reached out to both the FBI and Rick's team for clarification. Hey, better safe than sorry ... right?!?

          <li class="social__item social__item--3items">
           <a class="btn social__btn social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-footer","pos":1}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:9802468f-fee4-4ac1-9fa5-00aa8aec8509" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/fbi-needs-help-identify-capitol-rioter-looks-like-rick-moranis/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Ffbi-needs-help-identify-capitol-rioter-looks-like-rick-moranis%2F&amp;text=FBI%20Needs%20Help%20ID%27ing%20a%20Capitol%20Rioter%20Who%20Looks%20Like%20Rick%20Moranis&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-67538814-deea-40ec-89d1-65a87f7dc3a0">
       <div class="article__channel--viral">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":2}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:67538814-deea-40ec-89d1-65a87f7dc3a0" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/kylie-jenner-backlash-raise-money-makeup-artist-samuel-60k/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Kylie Jenner
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Catches Flak for Raising Cash ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           For Injured MUA Pal
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":2}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:67538814-deea-40ec-89d1-65a87f7dc3a0" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/kylie-jenner-backlash-raise-money-makeup-artist-samuel-60k/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fkylie-jenner-backlash-raise-money-makeup-artist-samuel-60k%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             1.5K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":2}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:67538814-deea-40ec-89d1-65a87f7dc3a0" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/kylie-jenner-backlash-raise-money-makeup-artist-samuel-60k/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fkylie-jenner-backlash-raise-money-makeup-artist-samuel-60k%2F&amp;text=Kylie%20Jenner%20Catches%20Flak%20for%20Trying%20to%20Raise%20Money%20for%20Injured%20MUA&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/21/2021 10:54 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-03c94a02c1c78cd7a2af67a3956dad34">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/5e/4by3/2021/03/21/5e3f9e80b566471b9a58ba40ee814613_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-03c94a02c1c78cd7a2af67a3956dad34-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6a44c9cb82d8f7f2ca42b2e4e681523d">
         <p>
          The old adage is true -- no good deed goes unpunished ... and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/kylie-jenner/">
           <strong>
            Kylie Jenner
           </strong>
          </a>
          is learning that first-hand this week after trying to do something nice for somebody she cares about.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6a44c9cb82d8f7f2ca42b2e4e681523d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-37ae006b5f36e8070de5fec68672ee96">
         <p>
          Get a load of this ... Kylie promoted a GoFundMe a few days ago for a celeb makeup artist named
          <strong>
           Samuel Rauda
          </strong>
          , who's worked with tons of famous people like
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bella-thorne/">
           <strong>
            Bella Thorne
           </strong>
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bebe-rexha/">
           <strong>
            Bebe Rexha
           </strong>
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/olivia-culpo/">
           <strong>
            Olivia Culpo
           </strong>
          </a>
          ,
          <strong>
           Doja Cat
          </strong>
          and many more. Kylie knows him too, apparently.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-37ae006b5f36e8070de5fec68672ee96-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-95e15f31e42172dffee225611055d155">
         <p>
          Sam was recently in a bad car accident that left him with major brain injuries and in need of surgeries. He's in the hospital now -- and, of course, his medical bills are certain to be immense ... so his family started a fundraiser, and his celeb clients have been plugging it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-95e15f31e42172dffee225611055d155-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-8066342dc2917d34f95ce9f7bf3de0dc">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/f6/4by3/2021/03/21/f6240380dd6346ebbb8bb2e44c03878b_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8066342dc2917d34f95ce9f7bf3de0dc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c6fe405f142cf10963c39a5d67bc85a5">
         <p>
          Kylie wanted to get the word out as well, so she posted something on her IG story that led folks to the GFM, asking anyone who wanted or could to donate ... while also sending kind words to Sam and his loved ones. She also donated herself -- $5,000.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c6fe405f142cf10963c39a5d67bc85a5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d4c54413e1bcf32a8cffa2d292802c0f">
         <p>
          The OG target amount was around $60k -- but it has since been bumped because of the flood of donations that have poured in. The fund has raised north of $97k as of now.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d4c54413e1bcf32a8cffa2d292802c0f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-c44ddf7662ca355195c576bbc138708c">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/68/4by3/2021/03/21/68f0243773354260a7589fbd1a952862_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            gofundme.com
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c44ddf7662ca355195c576bbc138708c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6e4854e9b902ce9081b9273d809f8dc4">
         <p>
          Innocent enough, right? WRONG!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! At least that's what Twitter justice warriors are saying a whole three to four days later ... giving her s*** for having the audacity to ask her followers to chip in, even though she's incredibly wealthy and could technically cover his fees on her own. That's the outrage -- with the main criticism being ... "she's out of touch."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6e4854e9b902ce9081b9273d809f8dc4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d5718d54fc2546f2ec62bddc2250559b">
         <p>
          For starters, anyone who follows Kylie and saw this wasn't forced/obligated to do anything. Second ... the logic that rich people/celebs are heartless heathens for trying to raise money when they could just as easily fund the whole damn thing is absurd. Hardly any celeb does that -- even the richest among them -- and it's unreasonable to expect them to anyway.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d5718d54fc2546f2ec62bddc2250559b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-dd5653cd41afd3eec55c5dc4979a7d47">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/f7/4by3/2021/03/21/f7281bd8dff74662b2a5f8082ebb9707_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            gofundme.com
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dd5653cd41afd3eec55c5dc4979a7d47-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ed95d58dce34c821d843a5a3903dfc48">
         <p>
          By that rationale ... every issue in the world should be remedied with celebrities' bank accounts, which is silly. Point is, Kylie donated ... and so did a bunch of others. It's possible she also kicked in even more anonymously or offered help elsewhere -- WE DON'T KNOW.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ed95d58dce34c821d843a5a3903dfc48-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8312786f733742fa7b33900288e81355">
         <p>
          Kylie, specifically, is dealing with this horse crap is because she's
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/03/05/kylie-jenner-officially-world-youngest-billionaire-forbes/">
           <strong>
            pegged a billionaire
           </strong>
          </a>
          . So with that in mind -- she should probably consider keeping these sorts of things on the DL ...  because people are downright ridiculous. And if she DGAF, even better. Do you, boo boo.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8312786f733742fa7b33900288e81355-->
       </div>

       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":3}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:ce169f91-d7bc-434b-b54e-9ba7b7c1a162" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/johnny-depp-home-broken-into-man-makes-drink-takes-shower/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Johnny Depp
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-none h2">
           Home Intruder Gets Comfy
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           ... Makes a Drink, Takes a Shower!!!
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":3}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:ce169f91-d7bc-434b-b54e-9ba7b7c1a162" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/johnny-depp-home-broken-into-man-makes-drink-takes-shower/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fjohnny-depp-home-broken-into-man-makes-drink-takes-shower%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-01c884121c7dc52b967b0d6ef6768702">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/71/4by3/2021/03/19/71e4b6a825ac4c9c8a32852600da9114_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty/Alamy
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-01c884121c7dc52b967b0d6ef6768702-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c4bf20ddb6076bdfecd8f62d15ea8cb9">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/johnny-depp/">
           <strong>
            Johnny Depp
           </strong>
          </a>
          's pad's apparently been a hot spot for unwelcome visitors this year ... and cops say the latest one really made himself at home.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c4bf20ddb6076bdfecd8f62d15ea8cb9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-040ebb15c50c24d217eed3360f955ab6">
         <p>
          Law enforcement sources tell TMZ ... cops got called to the actor's Hollywood Hills residence Thursday by a neighbor who spotted an apparently homeless man hanging out in the neighbor's backyard near the pool.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-040ebb15c50c24d217eed3360f955ab6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-18f545aaafd6fb0d6032c93fd4753e25">
         <p>
          The neighbor told police the man took off when confronted and hopped a gate ... which actually got him closer to Johnny's house.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-18f545aaafd6fb0d6032c93fd4753e25-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-a76b4f1607ba6d0e5a31e09dd686d206">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/a0/4by3/2021/03/19/a0baeb64282b4e5aaa4f74f42377632a_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Alamy
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a76b4f1607ba6d0e5a31e09dd686d206-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-fe0c6e79f5e41f3f9d76db1eb0b5dd65">
         <p>
          Our sources say shortly afterward, police were called again ... this time by Depp's security team alerting them someone was inside his home.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fe0c6e79f5e41f3f9d76db1eb0b5dd65-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-87549d0a75b963b0846fcdbbfc2f0d39">
         <p>
          When cops arrived, we're told they found the man taking a shower in one of the bathrooms ... and he refused to come out. So, cops had to kick the door down to arrest him.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-87549d0a75b963b0846fcdbbfc2f0d39-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c52b1561d689fcb70e401cbf2b2c3a63">
         <p>
          Along with the shower, the intruder also allegedly got into Depp's booze stash and made himself a drink. We're told he got booked for felony vandalism due to a damaged door in the home.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c52b1561d689fcb70e401cbf2b2c3a63-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-db213ec2ed6d100fe27c34f529e935ba">
         <p>
          We broke the story ... cops
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/07/johnny-depp-hollywood-hills-alleged-burglar-home/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <strong>
            arrested a female intruder
           </strong>
          </a>
          at Johnny's home back in January on suspicion of burglary.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-db213ec2ed6d100fe27c34f529e935ba-->

        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":4}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:a5bbb9f3-886a-457e-a088-a740952d863b" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/texas-roadhouse-founder-kent-taylor-commits-covid-related-suicide/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Texas Roadhouse Founder
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Commits COVID-Related Suicide
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":4}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:a5bbb9f3-886a-457e-a088-a740952d863b" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/texas-roadhouse-founder-kent-taylor-commits-covid-related-suicide/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Ftexas-roadhouse-founder-kent-taylor-commits-covid-related-suicide%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":4}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:a5bbb9f3-886a-457e-a088-a740952d863b" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/texas-roadhouse-founder-kent-taylor-commits-covid-related-suicide/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Ftexas-roadhouse-founder-kent-taylor-commits-covid-related-suicide%2F&amp;text=Texas%20Roadhouse%20Founder%20Kent%20Taylor%20Commits%20COVID-Related%20Suicide&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">

         3/21/2021 7:48 AM PT
        </h5>

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-f69c1bf23f22b152485be93bf5246681">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/5e/4by3/2021/03/21/5e8bfe22d46843aeac2710ac4f6fbdbe_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Breaking News
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f69c1bf23f22b152485be93bf5246681-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d309505a84ea21e283ea1e154b7bfd65">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Kent Taylor
          </strong>
          , the man who founded the wildly successful Texas Roadhouse restaurant chain, has taken his own life after experiencing severe, post-COVID side effects.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d309505a84ea21e283ea1e154b7bfd65-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a7d669dc00269f04703ab052c1f9f373">
         <p>
          Taylor suffered from tinnitus -- ringing in the ears -- which his family says greatly intensified in the last days of his life and ultimately became unbearable. At its worst, tinnitus can sound like a jet engine roaring inside the ears.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a7d669dc00269f04703ab052c1f9f373-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d2755d9f0a30f2a523c5276f75d9aa94">
         <p>
          The family said, "Kent battled and fought hard," but ultimately the suffering became too great.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d2755d9f0a30f2a523c5276f75d9aa94-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-89dfc483a85cf582a544754c738836fe">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/af/4by3/2021/03/21/af710a02967748709dc5186b2f1f399a_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-89dfc483a85cf582a544754c738836fe-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d23a46c9596d59e8b948cb9580bd5c63">
         <p>
          Kent was a master businessman, who founded Texas Roadhouse back in 1993. He came up with the idea on a cocktail napkin and brought it to life with the first restaurant located in Louisville, Kentucky. The plan took hold, and eventually, there were 537 Texas Roadhouses in 49 states, with 10 international locations.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d23a46c9596d59e8b948cb9580bd5c63-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-9d1c571cf8c9e1c63f94d05d270440c7">
         <p>
          Kent got national attention last Spring when he earmarked his entire salary to help support frontline workers during the pandemic.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9d1c571cf8c9e1c63f94d05d270440c7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-493fc58328a7ad16e55f5116cfd06a49">
         <p>
          He suffered from tinnitus, but it apparently flared up in a big way after he contracted COVID.   There's data indicating tinnitus is exacerbated by coronavirus.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-493fc58328a7ad16e55f5116cfd06a49-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8452c68b5dfc743b43cf49c581d3215f">
         <p>
          Louisville Mayor
          <strong>
           Greg Fischer
          </strong>
          said, "He was a maverick entrepreneur who embodied the values of never giving up and putting others first."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8452c68b5dfc743b43cf49c581d3215f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b19b6896413a60cf38083575567ca340">
         <p>
          Kent was 65.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b19b6896413a60cf38083575567ca340-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ac8deb4702ed71f2eef29b57aaf0cc16">
         <p>
          RIP.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ac8deb4702ed71f2eef29b57aaf0cc16-->
       </div>

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-29af9110-82a1-4eff-bc12-1264ef1f8a72">
       <div class="article__channel--reporting">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:29af9110-82a1-4eff-bc12-1264ef1f8a72" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/black-child-forced-to-kneel-apologize-white-headmaster/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Long Island School Scandal
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-titlecase h2">
           White Headmaster Confronts Black Student
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           Kneel and Apologize
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:29af9110-82a1-4eff-bc12-1264ef1f8a72" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/black-child-forced-to-kneel-apologize-white-headmaster/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fblack-child-forced-to-kneel-apologize-white-headmaster%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             10.6K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:29af9110-82a1-4eff-bc12-1264ef1f8a72" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/black-child-forced-to-kneel-apologize-white-headmaster/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fblack-child-forced-to-kneel-apologize-white-headmaster%2F&amp;text=Black%20Child%20Ordered%20To%20Kneel%20And%20Apologize%20To%20White%20Headmaster&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/21/2021 8:09 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-f92cd96c4e647fb4fd020429fafdf265">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/9d/4by3/2021/03/21/9db763edd2d94e8585ad21c0dd45753f_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Theodore Parisienne
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f92cd96c4e647fb4fd020429fafdf265-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d053316285b14fae6e472d9de12f9600">
         <p>
          The headmaster of a Long Island Catholic school reportedly made a black, 11-year-old student kneel and give him an apology.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d053316285b14fae6e472d9de12f9600-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1f2904fba4eb559b755c46a6e12aba4a">
         <p>
          An English teacher at the St. Martin de Porres Marianist school reportedly caught 6th grader
          <strong>
           Trayson Paul
          </strong>
          working on the wrong assignment in English class ... this according to the New York Daily News. The teacher reportedly ripped up his paper and sent him to the Headmaster's office.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1f2904fba4eb559b755c46a6e12aba4a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-7cd457df3580bb7a1d9b3afdbbac4a99">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/e5/4by3/2021/03/21/e58e33af059349ec9c11e00dfc4a2ecd_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Theodore Parisienne
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7cd457df3580bb7a1d9b3afdbbac4a99-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e65ff58c12c3879ac539835257bdea19">
         <p>
          Enter Headmaster
          <strong>
           John Holian
          </strong>
          , who allegedly told Trayson to get on his knees and confess his wrongdoing. Holian reportedly said he ordered the child to kneel because the father of a Nigerian student said it's the "African way" of apologizing.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e65ff58c12c3879ac539835257bdea19-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-bbe018a996f418ca23fcb33033e7bd54">
         <p>
          The boy's mother,
          <strong>
           Trisha Paul
          </strong>
          , says her son was humiliated and feared he was punished more harshly because of his race.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-bbe018a996f418ca23fcb33033e7bd54-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d6ff94542797e0f50890f2d0d7170176">
         <p>
          Paul told the Daily News ... “Once he started mentioning this African family, that’s when it just clicked. Like, this is not normal procedure. I felt there was no relevance at all. Is he generalizing that everyone who is Black is African? That’s when I realized something is not right with this situation.”
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d6ff94542797e0f50890f2d0d7170176-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-72b12db16c33c276bf0629142c24a417">
         <p>
          Holian is reportedly on temporary leave as the school investigates. We reached out to him but he said he would not comment on the situation.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-72b12db16c33c276bf0629142c24a417-->
       </div>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87-736069880-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-21-032121-south-beach-1057380/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:5d2a0267-9dd4-4d3e-8d33-20825a034e87',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>

          <p><strong>Twitter Tweet Unavailable</strong></p>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderTwitterTweetBlock() {
  var response = 'unknown';
  var target = document.getElementById('cb-d906fa98e3b5021d932ab9d15931c025-2128951678-target');

  function accept() {
    if (response === 'accepted') {
      return;
    }

    window.TMZ.utils.loadTwitterJs().then(function (twttr) {
      target.innerHTML = '';
      twttr.widgets.createTweet('1373424248321159173', target, {
        cards: '',
        conversation: '',
      });
    }).catch(reject);

    // there is no "accepted" html for twitter block, the above js does it all
    response = 'accepted';
  }

  function reject() {
    if (response === 'rejected') {
      return;
    }

    target.innerHTML = document.getElementById('cb-d906fa98e3b5021d932ab9d15931c025-2128951678-rejected').innerHTML;
    response = 'rejected';
  }

  watchConsent(function (canUse) {
    canUse('twitter') ? accept() : reject();
  });
});
         </script>

           <h3 class="poll-block__question">
            Whose Side You On?
           </h3>
          </a>
          <div id="poll-a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f-221884175-container">
           <div class="poll-block__answers">
            <div class="poll-block__message" style="display: none;">

            <form class="poll-block__form">

               <label class="poll-block__label">

                </span>

                 Prince Harry
                </span>
               </label>

              <li class="poll-block__list-item">

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderPoll() {
  var domId = 'poll-a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f-221884175';
  var pollRef = 'tmz:poll:a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f';
  var poll = {"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo:node:poll:1-0-0","_id":"a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f","status":"published","etag":"0ad16feeebc1d6a90c126f85741b8023","created_at":"1616191620571205","updated_at":"1616191673795907","title":"Stars 1 3\/19","question":"Whose Side You On?","question_url":"https:\/\/www.tmz.com\/2021\/03\/18\/prince-william-worried-harry-talks-american-tv-oprah-interview-lack-of-trust-gayle-king\/","allow_multiple_responses":true,"answers":[{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"c65b5166-10d2-4aa4-9095-14cb8daa16f6","title":"Prince Harry","initial_votes":0},{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"a5d70292-f3b4-49c2-8c80-d8069765d0bd","title":"Prince William","initial_votes":0}],"published_at":"2021-03-19T22:07:53.750503Z","order_date":"2021-03-19T22:07:53.750503Z"};
  var initialVotes = 0;
  poll.answers.forEach(function(answer) {
    initialVotes += answer.initial_votes;
  });

  var $container = $('#poll-a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f-221884175-container');
  var $answers = $container.find('.js-poll-answer');

  function removeRequired() {
    $answers.each(function() {
      $(this).off('click', removeRequired);
      $(this).removeAttr('required');
    });
  }

  $answers.each(function() {
    $(this).one('click', removeRequired);
  });

  function getTotalVotes(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = initialVotes;

    var answerIds = [];
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      answerIds.push($(this).data('answer-id'));
    });

    if (pollStats.answer_votes) {
      for (var key in pollStats.answer_votes) {
        if (answerIds.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
          totalVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[key];
        }
      }
    }

    return totalVotes;
  }

  function getPercentage(votes, total) {
    return total === 0 ? '0%' : Math.round(((votes / total) * 100)) + '%';
  }

  function renderResults(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = getTotalVotes(pollStats);
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      var answerId = $(this).data('answer-id');
      var answerVotes = poll.answers[$(this).data('answer-index')].initial_votes;
      if (pollStats.answer_votes && pollStats.answer_votes[answerId]) {
        answerVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[answerId];
      }
      $(this).text(getPercentage(answerVotes, totalVotes));
    });
    $container.find('.js-total-votes').text(totalVotes.toLocaleString() + ' total votes');
  }

  $container.find('form').one('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    $(this).submit(function(e) {
      // prevents multiple submissions
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $container.find('.js-vote-btn').val('Sending...').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

    function onCastVoteAccepted(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
      $container.html($('#poll-a67dde6c-2969-4606-8189-ee6e26dde97f-221884175-results-template').html());
      renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);

      var $toggler = $container.find('.poll-block__toggler');
      var $results = $container.find('.poll-block-results');
      var $disclaimer = $container.find('.poll-block-disclaimer');
      var isDisclaimerVisible = false;
      $toggler.click(function() {
        isDisclaimerVisible = !isDisclaimerVisible;
        if (!isDisclaimerVisible) {
          window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.getPollStats(domId, pollRef));
        }
        $toggler.text(isDisclaimerVisible ? 'Back to Poll Results' : '*Poll Results');
        $results.toggle();
        $disclaimer.toggle();
      });

      document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.GET_POLL_STATS_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {
        if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
          return;
        }
        renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);
      });
    }

    function onCastVoteRejected(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);
      $container.find('.poll-block__message').show();
      $container.find('.poll-block__btn').addClass('poll-block__btn--voted').css('cursor', 'auto');
    }

    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);

    var answerId = $(this).find(':checked').attr('value');
    window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.castVote(pollRef, answerId, domId));
  });
});
         </script>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderPoll() {
  var domId = 'poll-951d38a9-bbb5-4248-9c23-90513d32dcd1-1201202342';
  var pollRef = 'tmz:poll:951d38a9-bbb5-4248-9c23-90513d32dcd1';
  var poll = {"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo:node:poll:1-0-0","_id":"951d38a9-bbb5-4248-9c23-90513d32dcd1","status":"published","etag":"3cf439b481d617235d7c904d1f485939","created_at":"1616191796777286","updated_at":"1616191885417843","title":"Stars 3 3\/19","question":"Bigger Threat To U.S. ...","question_url":"https:\/\/www.tmz.com\/2021\/03\/18\/georgia-sheriff-out-spokesperson-atlanta-asian-spa-shooting-really-bad-day-comment-backlash\/","allow_multiple_responses":true,"answers":[{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"496c17e2-ff39-45da-af99-dab68bb2742e","title":"Russia","initial_votes":0},{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"60531ff5-0e59-4580-a619-dde603943518","title":"White Supremacists","initial_votes":0}],"published_at":"2021-03-19T22:11:25.372389Z","order_date":"2021-03-19T22:11:25.372389Z"};
  var initialVotes = 0;
  poll.answers.forEach(function(answer) {
    initialVotes += answer.initial_votes;
  });

  var $container = $('#poll-951d38a9-bbb5-4248-9c23-90513d32dcd1-1201202342-container');
  var $answers = $container.find('.js-poll-answer');

  function removeRequired() {
    $answers.each(function() {
      $(this).off('click', removeRequired);
      $(this).removeAttr('required');
    });
  }

  $answers.each(function() {
    $(this).one('click', removeRequired);
  });

  function getTotalVotes(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = initialVotes;

    var answerIds = [];
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      answerIds.push($(this).data('answer-id'));
    });

    if (pollStats.answer_votes) {
      for (var key in pollStats.answer_votes) {
        if (answerIds.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
          totalVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[key];
        }
      }
    }

    return totalVotes;
  }

  function getPercentage(votes, total) {
    return total === 0 ? '0%' : Math.round(((votes / total) * 100)) + '%';
  }

  function renderResults(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = getTotalVotes(pollStats);
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      var answerId = $(this).data('answer-id');
      var answerVotes = poll.answers[$(this).data('answer-index')].initial_votes;
      if (pollStats.answer_votes && pollStats.answer_votes[answerId]) {
        answerVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[answerId];
      }
      $(this).text(getPercentage(answerVotes, totalVotes));
    });
    $container.find('.js-total-votes').text(totalVotes.toLocaleString() + ' total votes');
  }

  $container.find('form').one('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    $(this).submit(function(e) {
      // prevents multiple submissions
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $container.find('.js-vote-btn').val('Sending...').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

    function onCastVoteAccepted(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
      $container.html($('#poll-951d38a9-bbb5-4248-9c23-90513d32dcd1-1201202342-results-template').html());
      renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);

      var $toggler = $container.find('.poll-block__toggler');
      var $results = $container.find('.poll-block-results');
      var $disclaimer = $container.find('.poll-block-disclaimer');
      var isDisclaimerVisible = false;
      $toggler.click(function() {
        isDisclaimerVisible = !isDisclaimerVisible;
        if (!isDisclaimerVisible) {
          window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.getPollStats(domId, pollRef));
        }
        $toggler.text(isDisclaimerVisible ? 'Back to Poll Results' : '*Poll Results');
        $results.toggle();
        $disclaimer.toggle();
      });

      document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.GET_POLL_STATS_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {
        if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
          return;
        }
        renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);
      });
    }

    function onCastVoteRejected(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);
      $container.find('.poll-block__message').show();
      $container.find('.poll-block__btn').addClass('poll-block__btn--voted').css('cursor', 'auto');
    }

    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);

    var answerId = $(this).find(':checked').attr('value');
    window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.castVote(pollRef, answerId, domId));
  });
});

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderPoll() {
  var domId = 'poll-396de768-d0b5-4977-958c-adb43e4a4419-1602866260';
  var pollRef = 'tmz:poll:396de768-d0b5-4977-958c-adb43e4a4419';
  var poll = {"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo:node:poll:1-0-0","_id":"396de768-d0b5-4977-958c-adb43e4a4419","status":"published","etag":"79ab1a680477b597f9df00ccf0b351a0","created_at":"1616192070400468","updated_at":"1616192104068422","title":"Stars 6 3\/19","question":"Gov. Andrew Cuomo ...","question_url":"https:\/\/www.tmz.com\/2021\/03\/16\/biden-cuomo-resign-if-sexual-harassment-allegations-confirmed\/","allow_multiple_responses":true,"answers":[{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"ca92f003-b39b-48b7-8095-38a5efdca2cd","title":"Resign","initial_votes":0},{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"88acb69e-712e-4e4b-abd5-509a1ab4a36d","title":"Stay Put","initial_votes":0}],"published_at":"2021-03-19T22:15:04.009017Z","order_date":"2021-03-19T22:15:04.009017Z"};
  var initialVotes = 0;
  poll.answers.forEach(function(answer) {
    initialVotes += answer.initial_votes;
  });

  var $container = $('#poll-396de768-d0b5-4977-958c-adb43e4a4419-1602866260-container');
  var $answers = $container.find('.js-poll-answer');

  function removeRequired() {
    $answers.each(function() {
      $(this).off('click', removeRequired);
      $(this).removeAttr('required');
    });
  }

  $answers.each(function() {
    $(this).one('click', removeRequired);
  });

  function getTotalVotes(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = initialVotes;

    var answerIds = [];
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      answerIds.push($(this).data('answer-id'));
    });

    if (pollStats.answer_votes) {
      for (var key in pollStats.answer_votes) {
        if (answerIds.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
          totalVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[key];
        }
      }
    }

    return totalVotes;
  }

  function getPercentage(votes, total) {
    return total === 0 ? '0%' : Math.round(((votes / total) * 100)) + '%';
  }

  function renderResults(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = getTotalVotes(pollStats);
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      var answerId = $(this).data('answer-id');
      var answerVotes = poll.answers[$(this).data('answer-index')].initial_votes;
      if (pollStats.answer_votes && pollStats.answer_votes[answerId]) {
        answerVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[answerId];
      }
      $(this).text(getPercentage(answerVotes, totalVotes));
    });
    $container.find('.js-total-votes').text(totalVotes.toLocaleString() + ' total votes');
  }

  $container.find('form').one('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    $(this).submit(function(e) {
      // prevents multiple submissions
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $container.find('.js-vote-btn').val('Sending...').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

    function onCastVoteAccepted(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
      $container.html($('#poll-396de768-d0b5-4977-958c-adb43e4a4419-1602866260-results-template').html());
      renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);

      var $toggler = $container.find('.poll-block__toggler');
      var $results = $container.find('.poll-block-results');
      var $disclaimer = $container.find('.poll-block-disclaimer');
      var isDisclaimerVisible = false;
      $toggler.click(function() {
        isDisclaimerVisible = !isDisclaimerVisible;
        if (!isDisclaimerVisible) {
          window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.getPollStats(domId, pollRef));
        }
        $toggler.text(isDisclaimerVisible ? 'Back to Poll Results' : '*Poll Results');
        $results.toggle();
        $disclaimer.toggle();
      });

      document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.GET_POLL_STATS_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {
        if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
          return;
        }
        renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);
      });
    }

    function onCastVoteRejected(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);
      $container.find('.poll-block__message').show();
      $container.find('.poll-block__btn').addClass('poll-block__btn--voted').css('cursor', 'auto');
    }

    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);

    var answerId = $(this).find(':checked').attr('value');
    window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.castVote(pollRef, answerId, domId));
  });
});
         </script>

          <div class="poll-block-results-container">
    <div class="poll-block-results">

                  <li class="poll-block-results__list-item">
            <span class="poll-block-results__pct" data-answer-id="054d659a-d201-428c-a5c6-d1f16e3fd1ec" data-answer-index="0"></span>
                          <span class="poll-block-results__answer">Arnold Schwarzenegger</span>
                      </li>
                  <li class="poll-block-results__list-item">
            <span class="poll-block-results__pct" data-answer-id="960b7079-908d-4dce-a9d3-93857376c149" data-answer-index="1"></span>

    <div class="poll-block-disclaimer" style="display: none;">

         <div class="poll-block">
          <a class="poll-block__link" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/18/arnold-schwarzenegger-voted-leader-against-alien-invasion-will-smith-second/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
           <h3 class="poll-block__question">
            Who's Best To Fight Alien Invasion?
           </h3>
          </a>
          <div id="poll-f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f-1884354188-container">

             Something Went Wrong

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderPoll() {
  var domId = 'poll-f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f-1884354188';
  var pollRef = 'tmz:poll:f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f';
  var poll = {"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo:node:poll:1-0-0","_id":"f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f","status":"published","etag":"2206dc99a1c487951551e6329307c81a","created_at":"1616192263003915","updated_at":"1616192320573815","title":"Stars 9 3\/19","question":"Who's Best To Fight Alien Invasion?","question_url":"https:\/\/www.tmz.com\/2021\/03\/18\/arnold-schwarzenegger-voted-leader-against-alien-invasion-will-smith-second\/","allow_multiple_responses":true,"answers":[{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"054d659a-d201-428c-a5c6-d1f16e3fd1ec","title":"Arnold Schwarzenegger","initial_votes":0},{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"960b7079-908d-4dce-a9d3-93857376c149","title":"Chris Evans","initial_votes":0}],"published_at":"2021-03-19T22:18:40.527706Z","order_date":"2021-03-19T22:18:40.527706Z"};
  var initialVotes = 0;
  poll.answers.forEach(function(answer) {
    initialVotes += answer.initial_votes;
  });

  var $container = $('#poll-f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f-1884354188-container');
  var $answers = $container.find('.js-poll-answer');

  function removeRequired() {
    $answers.each(function() {
      $(this).off('click', removeRequired);
      $(this).removeAttr('required');
    });
  }

  $answers.each(function() {
    $(this).one('click', removeRequired);
  });

  function getTotalVotes(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = initialVotes;

    var answerIds = [];
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      answerIds.push($(this).data('answer-id'));
    });

    if (pollStats.answer_votes) {
      for (var key in pollStats.answer_votes) {
        if (answerIds.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
          totalVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[key];
        }
      }
    }

    return totalVotes;
  }

  function getPercentage(votes, total) {
    return total === 0 ? '0%' : Math.round(((votes / total) * 100)) + '%';
  }

  function renderResults(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = getTotalVotes(pollStats);
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      var answerId = $(this).data('answer-id');
      var answerVotes = poll.answers[$(this).data('answer-index')].initial_votes;
      if (pollStats.answer_votes && pollStats.answer_votes[answerId]) {
        answerVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[answerId];
      }
      $(this).text(getPercentage(answerVotes, totalVotes));
    });
    $container.find('.js-total-votes').text(totalVotes.toLocaleString() + ' total votes');
  }

  $container.find('form').one('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    $(this).submit(function(e) {
      // prevents multiple submissions
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $container.find('.js-vote-btn').val('Sending...').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

    function onCastVoteAccepted(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
      $container.html($('#poll-f13d87b0-cb2d-48f0-a45f-bd48c2bc3d4f-1884354188-results-template').html());
      renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);

      var $toggler = $container.find('.poll-block__toggler');
      var $results = $container.find('.poll-block-results');
      var $disclaimer = $container.find('.poll-block-disclaimer');
      var isDisclaimerVisible = false;
      $toggler.click(function() {
        isDisclaimerVisible = !isDisclaimerVisible;
        if (!isDisclaimerVisible) {
          window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.getPollStats(domId, pollRef));
        }
        $toggler.text(isDisclaimerVisible ? 'Back to Poll Results' : '*Poll Results');
        $results.toggle();
        $disclaimer.toggle();
      });

      document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.GET_POLL_STATS_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {
        if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
          return;
        }
        renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);
      });
    }

    function onCastVoteRejected(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);
      $container.find('.poll-block__message').show();
      $container.find('.poll-block__btn').addClass('poll-block__btn--voted').css('cursor', 'auto');
    }

    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);

    var answerId = $(this).find(':checked').attr('value');
    window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.castVote(pollRef, answerId, domId));
  });
});
         </script>

          </strong>
          -- and we do mean in question because a Doritos truck wrapped in one gigantic advertisement is not exactly your run-of-the-mill Honda on the road.
         </p>

         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Sandra Oh
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-titlecase h2">
           'I Am Proud to Be Asian'
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           'I Belong Here!!!'
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":9}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:12b29746-e23c-4bab-a439-5b9565b36763" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/21/sandra-oh-gives-impassioned-stop-asian-hate-speech-in-pittsburgh/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F21%2Fsandra-oh-gives-impassioned-stop-asian-hate-speech-in-pittsburgh%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-29c3c7838bfcac856c62bef2e38caee0">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/b6/4by3/2021/03/21/b69beaeefa5f4060a9eda11cde6e3c33_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-29c3c7838bfcac856c62bef2e38caee0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-72722d72023e15cbdfb2921c5db5182c">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/sandra-oh/">
           <strong>
            Sandra Oh
           </strong>
          </a>
          spoke about fear in the Asian community for only about a minute-and-a-half, but it was emotional and downright stirring.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-72722d72023e15cbdfb2921c5db5182c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7b26627e5319342d735921f018d10031">
         <p>
          Sandra grabbed a bullhorn and addressed a crowd in Pittsburgh Saturday at the Stop Asian Hate Rally in the wake of the Atlanta massacre, and her words fired up the crowd.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7b26627e5319342d735921f018d10031-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default" id="cb-927bae102a48dfa79ec10d7586cb0e4e">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-927bae102a48dfa79ec10d7586cb0e4e-196836979-target">
          <blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
           <p dir="ltr" lang="en">
            BREAKING: Sandra Oh speaks at a “Stop Asian Hate” demonstration in Oakland to about 250 people.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            “I am proud to be Asian,” she says. “We belong here.”
            <a href="https://t.co/BCAtBpn4QQ">
             pic.twitter.com/BCAtBpn4QQ
            </a>
           </p>
           — Rebecca Johnson (@rebeccapaigejo)
           <a href="https://twitter.com/rebeccapaigejo/status/1373343182587584518?ref_src=twsrc^tfw">
            March 20, 2021
           </a>
           <a href="https://twitter.com/rebeccapaigejo" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
            @rebeccapaigejo
           </a>
          </blockquote>
         </div>
         <script id="cb-927bae102a48dfa79ec10d7586cb0e4e-196836979-rejected" type="text/x-consent-element">
          <p><strong>Twitter Tweet Unavailable</strong></p>
         </script>
         <script>

      });
    }).catch(reject);

         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-927bae102a48dfa79ec10d7586cb0e4e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ea43fe327186db70c1533f051a96c551">
         <p>
          She acknowledged the fear ... saying, "many in our community are very scared," and telling them the way to blunt that is to stand strong as a community.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ea43fe327186db70c1533f051a96c551-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-eaa46b89296d7184b63a448af456bd95">
         <p>
          She also noted the violence this past week was the first time her community could rise up to express fear and anger.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-eaa46b89296d7184b63a448af456bd95-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-550c1900e867c479901583bf01375be4">
         <p>
          And then, her call to action ... "To everyone here ... I will challenge everyone here, if you see something, will you help me? If you see one of our sisters and brothers in need, will you help us?" she continues, as people yell back, "Yes!" "We must understand, as Asian-Americans, we just need to reach out our hand to our sisters and brothers and say, 'Help me and I'm here.'"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-550c1900e867c479901583bf01375be4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4e1646d92300c08558184dfbe4b30245">
         <p>
          Sandra inspired the crowd with a chant ... "I am proud to be Asian! I belong here!"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4e1646d92300c08558184dfbe4b30245-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-09fa5d75f2ef9bd26f81ed981725b84d">
         <p>
          Watch the video ... it's pretty inspiring.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-09fa5d75f2ef9bd26f81ed981725b84d-->
