         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996-647846375-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-21-032121-kevin-hart-1057381/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:ed363e21-bfce-4489-84e6-ab513b5ba996',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195-398506334-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-19-031921-abby-lee-miller-1057289/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:c5ba0930-d9e3-480d-9257-a35ee8499195',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-85e7418199e8295b627b11fa2b780ee8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b53375ecdd83f179c23cd414367b6147">
         <p>

            Abby Lee Miller
           </strong>
          </a>
          says her dancing tip for

           <strong>
            Britney Spears
           </strong>
          </a>
          was well-intentioned, and she thinks Brit would understand ... and Abby's offering more advice if she wants it!
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          The "Dance Moms" star tells TMZ ... she loves Britney and just wants her to be her best, which is why she critiqued the singer's video with "Close your rib cage!" ... a recommendation she says is pretty basic stuff in the dance world.
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          Abby explains she had much more to share, but decided to keep it simple because she knows Britney's going through a lot ... but she
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/19/britney-spears-dance-form-attacked-by-abby-lee-miller/">

          "name": "TMZ",
          "logo": {
            "@type": "ImageObject",
            "url": "https://static.tmz.com/tmz-web/img/tmz-logo-red-147x60-v1.png",
            "height": 60,
            "width": 147
          }
        }
      }
         </script>
         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb-574199027-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-19-031921-lamar-odom-1057257/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:95a9c061-eaef-4434-ad95-6727b4a539bb',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c-199950886-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-19-031921-zak-bagans-crash-1056960/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:7830b98d-3b23-49e9-899b-9147fcf2aa8c',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

         <script id="poll-8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce-454035837-results-template" type="text/x-poll-element">
          <div class="poll-block-results-container">
    <div class="poll-block-results">
      <ul class="poll-block-results__list">
                  <li class="poll-block-results__list-item">
            <span class="poll-block-results__pct" data-answer-id="1ff846de-4b9c-4d29-99fb-7516384be73e" data-answer-index="0"></span>
                          <span class="poll-block-results__answer">Good Genes</span>
                      </li>
                  <li class="poll-block-results__list-item">
            <span class="poll-block-results__pct" data-answer-id="5d1da26a-b816-4fa6-85fc-a07c80eb4a54" data-answer-index="1"></span>
                          <span class="poll-block-results__answer">Good Docs</span>
                      </li>
              </ul>
    </div>
    <div class="poll-block-disclaimer" style="display: none;">
      <p class="poll-block-disclaimer__body">
        <strong>NOTE:</strong> Poll results are not scientific and reflect
        the opinions of only those users who chose to participate. Poll

         <div class="poll-block">
          <h3 class="poll-block__question">
           Gary Oldman ...
          </h3>
          <div id="poll-8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce-454035837-container">
           <div class="poll-block__answers">
            <div class="poll-block__message" style="display: none;">
             Something Went Wrong
            </div>
            <form class="poll-block__form">
             <ul class="poll-block__list">
              <li class="poll-block__list-item">
               <label class="poll-block__label">
                <input class="poll-block__input js-poll-answer" name="answer_id" required="" type="radio" value="1ff846de-4b9c-4d29-99fb-7516384be73e"/>
                <span class="poll-block__input-icon">
                </span>
                <span class="poll-block__input-label">
                 Good Genes
                </span>
               </label>
              </li>
              <li class="poll-block__list-item">
               <label class="poll-block__label">
                <input class="poll-block__input js-poll-answer" name="answer_id" required="" type="radio" value="5d1da26a-b816-4fa6-85fc-a07c80eb4a54"/>
                <span class="poll-block__input-icon">
                </span>
                <span class="poll-block__input-label">
                 Good Docs
                </span>
               </label>

             </ul>
             <input class="poll-block__btn js-vote-btn" type="submit" value="VOTE"/>
            </form>
           </div>

         </div>
         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderPoll() {
  var domId = 'poll-8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce-454035837';
  var pollRef = 'tmz:poll:8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce';
  var poll = {"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo:node:poll:1-0-0","_id":"8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce","status":"published","etag":"1cd693a9e5bce3ce7d85ca9144af0c03","created_at":"1616103541393421","updated_at":"1616103557123147","title":"0318-gary-oldman-genes-docs-poll","question":"Gary Oldman ...","allow_multiple_responses":true,"answers":[{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"1ff846de-4b9c-4d29-99fb-7516384be73e","title":"Good Genes","initial_votes":0},{"_schema":"pbj:tmz:apollo::poll-answer:1-0-0","_id":"5d1da26a-b816-4fa6-85fc-a07c80eb4a54","title":"Good Docs","initial_votes":0}],"published_at":"2021-03-18T21:39:17.062020Z","order_date":"2021-03-18T21:39:17.062020Z"};
  var initialVotes = 0;
  poll.answers.forEach(function(answer) {
    initialVotes += answer.initial_votes;
  });

  var $container = $('#poll-8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce-454035837-container');
  var $answers = $container.find('.js-poll-answer');

  function removeRequired() {
    $answers.each(function() {
      $(this).off('click', removeRequired);
      $(this).removeAttr('required');
    });
  }

  $answers.each(function() {
    $(this).one('click', removeRequired);
  });

  function getTotalVotes(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = initialVotes;

    var answerIds = [];
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      answerIds.push($(this).data('answer-id'));
    });

    if (pollStats.answer_votes) {
      for (var key in pollStats.answer_votes) {
        if (answerIds.indexOf(key) !== -1) {
          totalVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[key];
        }
      }
    }

    return totalVotes;
  }

  function getPercentage(votes, total) {
    return total === 0 ? '0%' : Math.round(((votes / total) * 100)) + '%';
  }

  function renderResults(pollStats) {
    var totalVotes = getTotalVotes(pollStats);
    $container.find('[data-answer-id]').each(function() {
      var answerId = $(this).data('answer-id');
      var answerVotes = poll.answers[$(this).data('answer-index')].initial_votes;
      if (pollStats.answer_votes && pollStats.answer_votes[answerId]) {
        answerVotes += pollStats.answer_votes[answerId];
      }
      $(this).text(getPercentage(answerVotes, totalVotes));
    });
    $container.find('.js-total-votes').text(totalVotes.toLocaleString() + ' total votes');
  }

  $container.find('form').one('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    $(this).submit(function(e) {
      // prevents multiple submissions
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $container.find('.js-vote-btn').val('Sending...').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

    function onCastVoteAccepted(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
      $container.html($('#poll-8685f78b-80ad-4ea2-a112-b2c35d2f65ce-454035837-results-template').html());
      renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);

      var $toggler = $container.find('.poll-block__toggler');
      var $results = $container.find('.poll-block-results');
      var $disclaimer = $container.find('.poll-block-disclaimer');
      var isDisclaimerVisible = false;
      $toggler.click(function() {
        isDisclaimerVisible = !isDisclaimerVisible;
        if (!isDisclaimerVisible) {
          window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.getPollStats(domId, pollRef));
        }
        $toggler.text(isDisclaimerVisible ? 'Back to Poll Results' : '*Poll Results');
        $results.toggle();
        $disclaimer.toggle();
      });

      document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.GET_POLL_STATS_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {
        if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
          return;
        }
        renderResults(e.detail.pollStats);
      });
    }

    function onCastVoteRejected(e) {
      if (e.detail.domId !== domId) {
        return;
      }

      document.removeEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);
      $container.find('.poll-block__message').show();
      $container.find('.poll-block__btn').addClass('poll-block__btn--voted').css('cursor', 'auto');
    }

    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_ACCEPTED, onCastVoteAccepted);
    document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.CAST_VOTE_REJECTED, onCastVoteRejected);

    var answerId = $(this).find(':checked').attr('value');
    window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.castVote(pollRef, answerId, domId));
  });
});
         </script>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7435ba26bd739c663883a11163345d90">
         <p>
          A Chicago Cubs prospect in their farm system got busted with a boatload of drugs -- so say police out of Colorado, who claim he was riding with a stash that would make Tony Montana blush.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7435ba26bd739c663883a11163345d90-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0a10572cdd5fb9f24b07bf88b81da1fb">
         <p>
          25-year-old
          <strong>
           Jesus Camargo-Corrales
          </strong>
          was reportedly arrested this past week near Vail, where a sheriff's deputy says he saw Camargo's car speeding and changing lanes erratically. After pulling him over, Camargo and his 2 passengers said they were driving to Denver from Phoenix. They then gave conflicting stories on where they were going -- police then searched the vehicle.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0a10572cdd5fb9f24b07bf88b81da1fb-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-38128ab859881b22c212693a320233e7">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/8d/4by3/2021/03/20/8d75951a92544fa09840bd67ca33ba18_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            AP
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-38128ab859881b22c212693a320233e7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-cf3549c21714fbe1bc1582093125b77a">
         <p>
          A K-9 unit is said to have been brought in ... and cops say it sniffed something in the trunk. Cops say they discovered a Cubs duffel bag, which they claim contained 21 pounds of methamphetamine and 1.2 pounds of oxycodone pills ... plus other paraphernalia.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-cf3549c21714fbe1bc1582093125b77a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-388841f40625845c44f83e7f38a7a73a">
         <p>
          An arrest affidavit claims that, at first, Camargo tried playing dumb ... but then later allegedly admitted he'd been contacted by someone in Sinaloa, Mexico to deliver this bag to Denver -- and copped to the fact that he knew there might've been drugs inside, per law enforcement.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-388841f40625845c44f83e7f38a7a73a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3b38cc4babffcf83133e117751b9a726">
         <p>
          As for what his alleged payoff was going to be -- according to Camargo, per police -- for this run ... just a measly $500!!!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3b38cc4babffcf83133e117751b9a726-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-6030a144f9b117a52050275ae2336511">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/d3/4by3/2021/03/20/d36e59cdb02748839b07cc6b3f8f7386_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            AP
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6030a144f9b117a52050275ae2336511-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-400439f3d49242e6b2b7a9b468097826">
         <p>
          He was arrested and booked on drug charges, including unlawful distribution and possession of methamphetamine and oxycodone -- class 1 and class 4 felonies, respectively. Camargo is reportedly still in custody as of Saturday. Unclear if he's been arraigned on the charges yet.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-400439f3d49242e6b2b7a9b468097826-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-439ec941918a75175fc4efa6112b1fbd">
         <p>
          The Cubs, for their part, say they're aware of the situation and are investigating the matter further -- refusing to comment beyond that. Camargo, a right-handed pitcher, was brought into the Cubs' farm system in 2014.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-439ec941918a75175fc4efa6112b1fbd-->
       </div>

Oldman","bio":"Gary Oldman is a talented British born movie actor who played Sid Vicious in Sid & Nancy, Drexl in True Romance, and George Smiley in Tinker Tailor Soldier Spy. He starred in Dawn of the Planet of the Apes and the remake of RoboCop. He is also an English filmmaker, musician and author. Renowned for his \"big\" acting style, Oldman is one of the most celebrated thespians of his generation, with a diverse career encompassing theatre, film and television.\n\nGary Oldman was born on March 21, 1958 in New Cross, London, England, the son of Kathleen (Cheriton), a homemaker, and Leonard Bertram Oldman, a welder.\n\nFor most of his career he was best-known for playing over-the-top antagonists such as the role of Russian terrorist Egor Korshunov in the 1997 blockbuster Air Force One, though he has recently reached a new audience with heroic roles in the Harry Potter and Dark Knight franchises. In amazing trivia, he was in Batman Begins and The Fifth Element.\n\nOldman won a scholarship to Britain's Rose Bruford Drama College, in Sidcup, Kent, where he received a B.A. in theatre arts in 1979. He subsequently studied with the Greenwich Young People's Theatre and went on to appear in a number of plays throughout the early '80s, including \"The Pope's Wedding,\" for which he received Time Out's Fringe Award for Best Newcomer of 1985-1986 and the British Theatre Association's Drama Magazine Award as Best Actor for 1985. Before fame, he was employed as a worker in assembly lines, and as a porter in an operating theater. He also got jobs selling shoes and beheading pigs while supporting his early acting career. He was also in the movie The Dark Knight with Heath Ledger.\n\nHis film debut was Remembrance (1982), though his most-memorable early role came when he played Sex Pistol Sid Vicious in the biopic Sid and Nancy (1986) picking up the Evening Standard Film Award as Best Newcomer. He then received a Best Actor nomination from BAFTA for his portrayal of '60s playwright Joe Orton in Prick Up Your Ears (1987).\n\nIn the 1990s, Oldman brought to life a series of iconic real-world and fictional villains including Lee Harvey Oswald in JFK (1991), the title character in Bram Stoker's Dracula (1992), Drexl Spivey in True Romance (1993), Stansfield in L\u00e9on: The Professional (1994), Jean-Baptiste Emanuel Zorg in The Fifth Element (1997) and Ivan Korshunov in Air Force One (1997). That decade also saw Oldman portraying Ludwig van Beethoven in biopic Immortal Beloved (1994).\n\nOldman scored the coveted role of Sirius Black in Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (2004), giving him a key part in one of the highest-grossing franchises ever. He reprised that role in Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (2005) and Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (2007). Oldman also took on the iconic role of Detective James Gordon in writer-director Christopher Nolan's Batman Begins (2005), a role he played again in The Dark Knight (2008) and The Dark Knight Rises (2012). Prominent film critic Mark Kermode, in reviewing The Dark Knight, wrote, \"the best performance in the film, by a mile, is Gary Oldman's ... it would be lovely to see him get a[n Academy Award] nomination because actually, he's the guy who gets kind of overlooked in all of this.\"\n\nOldman co-starred with Jim Carrey in the 2009 version of A Christmas Carol in which Oldman played three roles. He had a starring role in David Goyer's supernatural thriller The Unborn, released in 2009. In 2010, Oldman co-starred with Denzel Washington in The Book of Eli. He also played a lead role in Catherine Hardwicke's Red Riding Hood. Oldman voiced the role of villain Lord Shen and was nominated for an Annie Award for his performance in Kung Fu Panda 2.\n\nIn 2011, Oldman portrayed master spy George Smiley in the adaptation of John le Carr\u00e9's Tinker Tailor Soldier Spy (2011), and the role scored Oldman his first Academy Award nomination. In 2014, he played one of the lead humans in the science fiction action film Dawn of the Planet of the Apes (2014). Also in 2014, Oldman starred alongside Joel Kinnaman, Abbie Cornish, Michael Keaton, and Samuel L. Jackson in the remake of RoboCop (2014), as Norton, the scientist who creates RoboCop. Also that year, Oldman starred in Dawn of the Planet of the Apes as one of the leads alongside Jason Clarke and Keri Russell.\n\nAside from acting, Oldman tried his hand at writing and directing for Nil by Mouth (1997). The movie opened the Cannes Film Festival in 1997, and won Kathy Burke a Best Actress prize at the festival.\n\nOldman has three children - one with first wife Lesley Manville, and two with third wife Donya Fiorentino. He married Alexandra Edenborough on December 31, 2008 until they divorced in January 2015. He was married to actress Uma Thurman from 1990 to 1992. He married his fourth wife Alexandra Edenborough in 2008 but the couple divorced in 2015. He has three sons named Alfie, Gulliver and    <script>
    wbq.push(function manageSearchScreen() {
  var $search = $('.js__search-screen');
  var $searchCloseBtn = $('#search-screen-close-btn');
  var $searchToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--search-toggle');
  var $mastheadSearchOpenBtn = $('#masthead-search-open-btn');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockSearchFocus() {
    $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusSearchCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('search-screen'), event.target)) {
      $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockSearchFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
    $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
  }

  // close X used to dismiss mobile search overlay
  $searchToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    // Toggle search screen visibility
    $search.toggleClass('search-screen--is-open');

    if ($search.hasClass('search-screen--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockSearchFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('search-screen');
      $search.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockSearchFocus();
        $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $search.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
   </script>

  <script id="newsletter-subscription-success" type="text">
   <p class="thanks">Thank you!<br> You have successfully signed up.</p>
  </script>
  <script>
   wbq.push(function renderSubscribeToNewsletterModal() {
    function renderThankYou() {
      document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-form').innerHTML = document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-success').innerHTML;
      window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.destroyComponent('newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root', true));
    }

    function renderComponent(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      var lightboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
      var lightboxDivId = 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root';
      lightboxDiv.setAttribute('id', lightboxDivId);
      document.getElementById('lightbox-root').prepend(lightboxDiv);
      if (window.TMZ.utils.isValidEmail($('#newsletter-subscription-email').val())) {
        window.TMZ.renderComponent(
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox',
          {
            email: $('#newsletter-subscription-email').val(),
            id: 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          },
        );
        document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.SUBSCRIBE_TO_NEWSLETTER_ACCEPTED, renderThankYou);
      } else {
        alert('Please enter a valid email.');
      }
    }

    $('#newsletter-subscription-form').on('submit', renderComponent);
  });
  </script>
